<script>
    StackExchange.ready(function () {

        var location = 0;
        if ($("body").hasClass("questions-page")) {
            location = 1;;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("question-page")) {
            location = 1;;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("faq-page")) {
            location = 5;;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("home-page")) {
            location = 3;;
        }

        $('#tell-me-more').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("hero.action", { hero_action_type: 'cta', location: location }, true);
            });
        });
        $('#herobox #close').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("hero.action", { hero_action_type: "minimize", location: location }, true);
            });
            $.cookie("hero", "mini", { path: "/", expires: 365 });
            $.ajax({
                url: "/hero-mini",
                success: function (data) {
                    $("#herobox").fadeOut("fast", function () {
                        $("#herobox").replaceWith(data);
                        $("#herobox-mini").fadeIn("fast");
                    });
                }
            });
            return false;
        });
    });

</script>    <script>
        StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
            StackExchange.gps.track("hero.show", { hero_type: "hero", location: 3 }, true);
        });
    </script>

<section class="section--major" aria-label="We Sea Change">
<div class="row">
<div class="featured-video video-parent">
	<div href="" class="video-preview tile tile--link">
      <a class="box__content" href="/go/sea-change/" alt="We see inside the heads of 16th century Spanish explorers." >
	<figure>
		<img src="/media/university-of-west-florida/homepage/feature/sea-change-photo-features/WorthJohn_Environmental-Portrait.jpg" alt="Dr. John Worth, associate professor of anthropology, teaches historical archaeology, historical research methods, Southeastern Indians, and field and laboratory methods in archaeology." style="    " />
	</figure>
  </a>
  </div>	
	<div class="callout bg--blue bg--photo">
	
	<div class="callout__hgroup">
		<div class="callout__superhead">
			#WeSeaChange
		</div>
		
		<h2 class="callout__headline">
			We see inside the heads of 16th century Spanish explorers.
		</h2>
		
		<div class="callout__subhead">
			
		</div>
	</div>
	
	<div class="callout__body">
		<p>This is where they stepped ashore. Six years before the Spanish settlement in St. Augustine and 48 years before the English settlement in Jamestown, Spanish explorer Trist&aacute;n de Luna y Arellano led an expedition to colonize the northern Gulf Coast.</p>
<p>For the 13 professors and their students in UWF&rsquo;s archaeology program, it&rsquo;s a dream come true. It&rsquo;s real history, and it&rsquo;s right here.</p>
<div class="callout__subhead">&ndash;Division of Anthropology and Archaeology</div>
	</div>
	
			<figure>
			<img src="/media/university-of-west-florida/homepage/feature/sea-change-photo-features/NMP_090414_0750.png" alt="Textural background of branching trees" style="    " />
		</figure>
	</div>	
</div>

<script>
    StackExchange.ready(function () {

        var location = 0;
        if ($("body").hasClass("questions-page")) {
            location = 1;;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("question-page")) {
            location = 1;;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("faq-page")) {
            location = 5;;
        } else if ($("body").hasClass("home-page")) {
            location = 3;;
        }

        $('#tell-me-more').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("hero.action", { hero_action_type: 'cta', location: location }, true);
            });
        });
        $('#herobox #close').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("hero.action", { hero_action_type: "minimize", location: location }, true);
            });
            $.cookie("hero", "mini", { path: "/", expires: 365 });
            $.ajax({
                url: "/hero-mini",
                success: function (data) {
                    $("#herobox").fadeOut("fast", function () {
                        $("#herobox").replaceWith(data);
                        $("#herobox-mini").fadeIn("fast");
                    });
                }
            });
            return false;
        });
    });

</script>    <script>

            StackExchange.gps.track("hero.show", { hero_type: "hero", location: 3 }, true);
        });
    </script>

	<figure>
		<img src="/media/university-of-west-florida/homepage/feature/sea-change-photo-features/WorthJohn_Environmental-Portrait.jpg" alt="Dr. John Worth, associate professor of anthropology, teaches historical archaeology, historical research methods, Southeastern Indians, and field and laboratory methods in archaeology." style="    " />
	</figure>

	<div class="callout bg--blue bg--photo">
	
	<div class="callout__hgroup">
		<div class="callout__superhead">
			#WeSeaChange
		</div>
		
		<h2 class="callout__headline">
			We see inside the heads of 16th century Spanish explorers.
		</h2>
		
		<div class="callout__subhead">
			
		</div>
	</div>
	
	<div class="callout__body">
		<p>This is where they stepped ashore. Six years before the Spanish settlement in St. Augustine and 48 years before the English settlement in Jamestown, Spanish explorer Trist&aacute;n de Luna y Arellano led an expedition to colonize the northern Gulf Coast.</p>
<p>For the 13 professors and their students in UWF&rsquo;s archaeology program, it&rsquo;s a dream come true. It&rsquo;s real history, and it&rsquo;s right here.</p>
<div class="callout__subhead">&ndash;Division of Anthropology and Archaeology</div>
	</div>
	
			<figure>
			<img src="/media/university-of-west-florida/homepage/feature/sea-change-photo-features/NMP_090414_0750.png" alt="Textural background of branching trees" style="    " />
		</figure>
	</div>
